[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.TikaAppRUnpackerFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaAppRUnpackerFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:74[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.TikaAppRUnpackerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTikaAppRUnpackerFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:5[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: e329145bbb375a14[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA file path traversal vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFuzzerSecurityIssueCritical[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m has been detected[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min Apache Tika's file system emitter component during fuzzing. The vulnerability [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs when processing archive files with malicious path entries that attempt to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraverse outside the intended output directory using relative path sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`..[0m[35m/../../[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The issue manifests when extracting embedded documents from RUnpack [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives through the FileSystemEmitter, allowing potential unauthorized file system[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Overview[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe security issue is a **file path traversal vulnerability** detected by Jazzer's [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer during fuzzing operations. The exception is triggered when attempting to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite a file to a path that would escape the intended output directory structure: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp6295180230880069174/output/q/r/s/t/./input.bin/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-tr[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95maversal[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **path traversal** [0m[1;39m([0m[39malso known as directory traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m security [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability, classified as critical by the fuzzer. Path traversal vulnerabilities[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallow attackers to access files and directories stored outside the intended [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory by manipulating file path references with special character sequences [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuch as `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdot-dot-slash[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Attack Vector**: The malicious path contains both current directory references[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`.[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and parent directory traversal sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../../[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that, when resolved, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould write files outside the intended output directory structure.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following execution [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflow:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archive parsing begins with `PackageParser` processing entries[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `RUnpackExtractor` extracts embedded documents with their byte content[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `EmittingEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler` handles the extracted content[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mFileSystemEmitter.emit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` attempts to write the file to the file system[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The path validation in `[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` catches the malicious path[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Detection Point**: The Jazzer security sanitizer [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m successfully detected[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand blocked the traversal attempt at the `copyMismatchMvHook` method call, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing the actual file system write operation.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Affected Path**: The problematic path structure shows an attempt to traverse [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp6295180230880069174/output/q/r/s/t/./input.bin/[0m[39m` back three [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../../[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to write a file named `jazzer-traversal` in an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munauthorized location.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Components Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35madd[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m66[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How embedded document metadata [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is propagated to emitters[0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **PackageParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.parser.pkg.PackageParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Methods `[0m[1;35mparseEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m481[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mparseEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m386[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entry name extraction and processing from archive formats[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Path Handling in Pipes Framework**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe investigation should focus on determining where malicious path entries from [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Code Snippets in Relation to the Evaluation Report[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Location**: The path traversal vulnerability exists in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFileSystemEmitter.emit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboth overloaded versions at lines [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m98[0m[39m and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m146[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m165[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which lack validation before resolving paths and performing file [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Root Cause**: When `[0m[1;35mbasePath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called with a path containing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `.[0m[35m/input.bin/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, Java's Path [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI resolves these relative references, potentially escaping the intended [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`basePath` directory. No validation occurs before file operations proceed.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Attack Flow**: [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malicious archive entries with traversal sequences in their names flow through[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPackageParser → RUnpackExtractor → EmittingEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFileSystemEmitter[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The RESOURCE_NAME_KEY metadata field carries the unsanitized entry name[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `PATH_STRATEGY.EMBEDDED_PATH` is configured [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas in RecursivelyExtract [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCLI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, these names are used to construct file paths[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The insufficient sanitization in [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mAbstractEmbeddedDocumentBytesHandler.addSubDirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m102[0m[39m's regex `[0m[32m"\\.\\./"[0m[39m`  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplacement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fails to prevent all traversal patterns[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Reference Implementation**: The codebase already contains the correct [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation pattern in `FileSystemFetcher` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m67[0m[39m for `[0m[1;35misDescendant[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m82[0m[39m for fetching[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, demonstrating awareness of path traversal risks.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Dual [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Methods**: Both `[0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString, List<Metadata>, ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString, InputStream, Metadata, ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must continue to function for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir respective purposes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJSON metadata vs binary streams[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Directory Creation**: The logic to create parent directories when they don't [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexist must be preserved [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m92[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m149[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m150[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **ON_EXISTS Behavior**: The three strategies [0m[1;39m([0m[39mREPLACE, EXCEPTION, SKIP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling existing files must work correctly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m152[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Archive Structure Preservation**: When using `PATH_STRATEGY.EMBEDDED_PATH`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe legitimate directory structure from archives should be maintained [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminus [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal attempts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: Existing legitimate use cases with well-formed paths[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust continue to work.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Previous Patches Analysis[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis appears to be the first patch attempt for this vulnerability, as no previous [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch context is provided in the evaluation report.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Path Traversal Validation in FileSystemEmitter[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-pipes/tika-emitters/tika-emitter-fs/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/pipes/emitt[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mer/fs/FileSystemEmitter.java`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Add a private validation method to FileSystemEmitter class [0m[1;39m([0m[39minsert [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter line [0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * Validates that the resolved path is a descendant of basePath and does not [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontain[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * malicious patterns that could lead to path traversal attacks.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * @param path the relative path to validate and resolve[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * @return the validated resolved path[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * @throws TikaEmitterException if validation fails[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate Path [0m[1;35mvalidateAndResolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws TikaEmitterException [0m[1;39m{[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Basic validation[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath == null || [0m[1;35mpath.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mTikaEmitterException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"path must not be null or empty"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: The fix uses the same validation logic as [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFileSystemFetcher.isDescendant[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m67[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring consistency across the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Defense-in-Depth**: Multiple layers of validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull bytes, absolute paths,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provide robust protection against various attack vectors.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Non-Breaking**: Legitimate use cases continue to work while malicious paths [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare rejected with clear error messages.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Proper Use of Path API**: Uses `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of `[0m[1;35mtoRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` because[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe're creating new files that don't exist yet, avoiding IOException.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Clear Error Messages**: Provides actionable error messages for security [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mviolations, aiding in debugging and monitoring.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Directory Creation**: Validation occurs before directory creation, so [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate paths still get their parent directories created.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **ON_EXISTS Behavior**: The validation doesn't interfere with the existing file [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling strategies.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Path Strategy Support**: Both PATH_STRATEGY.ID and PATH_STRATEGY.EMBEDDED_PATH[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to work, but EMBEDDED_PATH now has proper security controls.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Archive Structure**: Legitimate directory structures from archives are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserved through the improved [0m[1;35maddSubDirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m sanitization.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Blocks Path Traversal**: The `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check on normalized paths catches [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall traversal attempts, including the fuzzer's [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`.[0m[35m/input.bin/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m` pattern.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Multiple Attack Vectors**: Protects against null byte injection, absolute path[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minjection, and relative path traversal.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **CLI Tool Security**: Fixes the vulnerability in RecursivelyExtract which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly uses EMBEDDED_PATH strategy.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Both [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Methods**: Applies validation to both overloaded [0m[1;35memit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m methods, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring comprehensive coverage.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Performance Impact**: Minimal - path normalization is efficient and only runs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce per file emission.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error Handling**: Code that previously succeeded with malicious paths will now[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow TikaEmitterException. This is the desired behavior but may affect error [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling in calling code. Mitigation: Clear exception messages help users [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand the security issue.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Edge Cases**: Symbolic links within basePath are not followed by [0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39munlike [0m[1;35mtoRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This is acceptable for the emitter use case and actually [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovides additional security.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: Legitimate paths continue to work. Only malicious [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths are rejected, which is the intended behavior change.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in the Codebase[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **FileSystemFetcher**: Lines [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m82[0m[39m show the same validation pattern for reading [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles, demonstrating this is the established pattern in Tika.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mFSUtil.resolveRelative[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Lines [0m[1;36m197[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m203[0m[39m show similar defensive programming [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor path resolution.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mFilenameUtils.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Lines [0m[1;36m97[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m show component-level sanitization that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwe leverage in the secondary fix.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe proposed fix aligns with existing security patterns in the Tika codebase while [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressing the specific vulnerability detected by the fuzzer.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
